<h3 data-start="258" data-end="301" class=""><strong data-start="262" data-end="301">Option 1: Use an AI Website Builder</strong></h3>
<p data-start="302" data-end="371" class="">These tools make the process super quick and easy—no coding required.</p>
<h4 data-start="373" data-end="403" class=""><strong data-start="378" data-end="403">Recommended AI Tools:</strong></h4>

<li data-start="404" data-end="641" class="">

<ul data-start="443" data-end="641">
<li data-start="443" data-end="495" class="">
<p data-start="445" data-end="495" class="">Made specifically for freelancers and contractors.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="499" data-end="576" class="">
<p data-start="501" data-end="576" class="">You just enter what you do, and it builds the whole site in under a minute.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="580" data-end="641" class="">
<p data-start="582" data-end="641" class="">You can edit the text, add your photo, and link to your CV.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li data-start="643" data-end="823" class="">
<p data-start="646" data-end="677" class=""><strong data-start="646" data-end="656">Framer</strong> (<a data-start="658" data-end="676" rel="noopener" target="_new" class="" href="https://framer.com/">https://framer.com</a>)</p>

</li>
<li data-start="712" data-end="768" class="">

</li>
<li data-start="772" data-end="823" class="">
<p data-start="774" data-end="823" class="">Great if you want a more polished, creative look.</p>
</li>

<p data-start="169" data-end="216" class=""><strong data-start="169" data-end="192">Kantoor-achtergrond</strong> (alsof je op werk bent)</p>
</li>
<li data-start="217" data-end="254" class="">
<p data-start="219" data-end="254" class=""><strong data-start="219" data-end="239">Stadsachtergrond</strong> (iets moderns)</p>
</li>
<li data-start="255" data-end="303" class="">
<p data-start="257" data-end="303" class=""><strong data-start="257" data-end="269">Vervagen</strong> (jezelf scherp, achtergrond vaag)</p>
</li>
<li data-start="304" data-end="362" class="">
<p data-start="306" data-end="362" class=""><strong data-start="306" data-end="327">Of iets creatiefs</strong>, zoals tech-vibes of donkere stijl</p>
</li>
</ul>

<h3 data-start="312" data-end="387" class="">Wil je <strong data-start="323" data-end="350">je echte gezicht houden</strong> en alleen de achtergrond veranderen?</h3>
<p data-start="388" data-end="421" class="">Dan kan ik dat ook voor je doen ✅</p>
<p data-start="423" data-end="444" class="">Stuur me gewoon even:</p>
<ul data-start="445" data-end="588">
<li data-start="445" data-end="526" class="">
<p data-start="447" data-end="526" class="">Of je een <strong data-start="457" data-end="466">witte</strong>, <strong data-start="468" data-end="479">kantoor</strong>- of <strong data-start="484" data-end="504">vage achtergrond</strong> wilt (of iets anders)</p>
</li>
<li data-start="527" data-end="588" class="">
<p data-start="529" data-end="588" class="">Of ik je bestaande foto moet gebruiken (die je net stuurde)</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p data-start="590" data-end="708" class="">Dan geef ik je een nieuwe foto mét je echte gezicht, netjes met de achtergrond die jij wilt. <hr data-start="193" data-end="196" class="">
<h3 data-start="198" data-end="255" class="">🔧 <strong data-start="205" data-end="255">Online Tools om zelf achtergrond te veranderen</strong></h3>
<h4 data-start="257" data-end="305" class="">✅ <strong data-start="264" data-end="305">1. <a data-start="269" data-end="303" rel="noopener" target="_new" class="" href="https://www.remove.bg/">Remove.bg</a></strong></h4>
<ul data-start="306" data-end="496">
<li data-start="306" data-end="358" class="">
<p data-start="308" data-end="358" class="">Verwijdert automatisch de achtergrond van je foto.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="359" data-end="428" class="">
<p data-start="361" data-end="428" class="">Daarna kun je een nieuwe achtergrond toevoegen (zoals een kantoor).</p>
</li>
<li data-start="429" data-end="496" class="">
<p data-start="431" data-end="496" class="">Super simpel: upload &gt; achtergrond weg &gt; kies nieuwe achtergrond.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h4 data-start="498" data-end="543" class="">✅ <strong data-start="505" data-end="543">2. <a data-start="510" data-end="541" rel="noopener" target="_new" class="" href="https://www.canva.com/">Canva</a></strong></h4>
<ul data-start="544" data-end="761">
<li data-start="544" data-end="574" class="">
<p data-start="546" data-end="574" class="">Maak een gratis account aan.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="575" data-end="656" class="">
<p data-start="577" data-end="656" class="">Upload je foto &gt; kies "Achtergrond verwijderen" (werkt gratis met proefversie).</p>
</li>
<li data-start="657" data-end="716" class="">
<p data-start="659" data-end="716" class="">Voeg dan een kantoor-achtergrond of eigen afbeelding toe.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="717" data-end="761" class="">
<p data-start="719" data-end="761" class="">Extra opties zoals vervagen, filters, etc.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h4 data-start="763" data-end="836" class="">✅ <strong data-start="770" data-end="836">3. <a data-start="775" data-end="834" rel="noopener" target="_new" class="">Fotor</a></strong></h4>
<ul data-start="837" data-end="951">
<li data-start="837" data-end="872" class="">
<p data-start="839" data-end="872" class="">Werkt vergelijkbaar met remove.bg</p>
</li>
<li data-start="873" data-end="906" class="">
<p data-start="875" data-end="906" class="">Gratis basisversie beschikbaar.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="907" data-end="951" class="">
<p data-start="909" data-end="951" class="">Ook geschikt voor zakelijke profielfoto's.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<hr data-start="953" data-end="956" class="">
<h3 data-start="958" data-end="973" class="">💡 <strong data-start="965" data-end="973">Tip:</strong></h3>
<p data-start="974" data-end="1068" class="">Wil je bijvoorbeeld <strong data-start="994" data-end="1037">een vage kantoorsetting als achtergrond</strong>? Zoek dan op stocksites zoals:</p>
<ul data-start="1069" data-end="1249">
<li data-start="1069" data-end="1130" class="">
<p data-start="1071" data-end="1130" class=""><a data-start="1071" data-end="1130" rel="noopener" target="_new" class="">Unsplash</a></p>
</li>
<li data-start="1131" data-end="1249" class="">
<p data-start="1133" data-end="1249" class=""><a data-start="1133" data-end="1193" rel="noopener" target="_new" class="">Pexels</a>
En upload die als nieuwe achtergrond in Canva of Fotor.</p>
</li>
</ul>
